 shodhakartaaon ne paaya ki jo log upnagaron main rahete hai ve gaanvon main or kasbon main rahane vaale logon kii apeksha adhik khush rahete hai
 Stress in marital life leads to fear of depression
 Professor Stephen Goetz at Pennsylvania State University in the United States said, "this is a real concern not only for the United Nations, but around the world
" ' adhyayan main pataa chalaa he ki maansik rup se aswasth log ek maah main 8

 Goetz said, 'people living in the suburbs are close to jobs and all the amenities that a large city can provide, but they are also far from the stress of towns
